    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        S 
        
       
      
        S
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">

         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0576em;">
          S
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     取平面
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        2

         − 
        
       
         z

         =

        2x - z - 1 = 0
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          2
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">

          z
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">

        <span class="base">

         </span>

         </span>

          0

       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     。为使
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        n 
        
       
      
        n
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">

     <span class="katex--inline">

        z

       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">

          z
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     分量 &gt; 0，取平面的法向量为
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        N 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         (

       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">
          N
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          −
         </span>
         <span class="mord">

         </span>
         <span class="mpunct">
          ,

         </span>
         <span class="mord">

         <span class="mpunct">
          ,
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          1
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，故单位法向量：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--display">
      <span class="katex-display">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         n 
         
        
          = 
         
         
          
          
            ( 
           
          
            − 
           
          
            2 
           
          
            , 
           
          
            0 
           
          
            , 
           
          
            1 
           
          
            ) 
           
          
          
           
            
            
              2 
             
            
              2 
             
            
           
             + 
            
            
            
              0 
             
            
              2 
             
            
           
             + 
            
            
            
              1 
             
            
              2 
             
            
           
          
         
        
          = 
         
         
          
          
            ( 
           
          
            − 
           
          
            2 
           
          
            , 
           
          
            0 
           
          
            , 
           
          
            1 
           
          
            ) 
           
          
          
          
            5 
           
          
         
        
          . 
         
        
       
         n = \frac{(-2, 0, 1)}{\sqrt{2^2 + 0^2 + 1^2}} = \frac{(-2, 0, 1)}{\sqrt{5}}.
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           n
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mrel">
           =
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 2.357em; vertical-align: -0.93em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mopen nulldelimiter">
           </span>
           <span class="mfrac">
            <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
             <span class="vlist-r">
              <span class="vlist" style="height: 1.427em;">
               <span class="" style="top: -2.1966em;">
                <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;">
                </span>
                <span class="mord">

    <p>
     【第三步：计算
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        ( 
        
       
         c 
        
       
         u 
        
       
         r 
        
       
         l 
        
       
         F 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
         ⋅ 
        
       
         n 
        
       
      
        (curl F) \cdot n
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          c
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          u
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0278em;">
          r
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">
          lF
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          ⋅
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          n
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     】
    </p>
    <p>
     由上，
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--display">
      <span class="katex-display">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         ( 
         
        
          c 
         
        
          u 
         
        
          r 
         
        
          l 
         
        
          F 
         
        
          ) 
         
        
          ⋅ 
         
        
          n 
         
        
          = 
         
        
          ( 
         
        
          z 
         
        
          − 
         
        
          2 
         
        
          x 
         
        
          ) 
         
        
          ( 
         
        
          x 
         
        
          , 
         
        
          − 
         
        
          3 
         
        
          y 
         
        
          , 
         
        
          z 
         
        
          ) 
         
        
          ⋅ 
         
         
          
          
            ( 
           
          
            − 
           
          
            2 
           
          
            , 
           
          
            0 
           
          
            , 
           
          
            1 
           
          
            ) 
           
          
          
          
            5 
           
          
         
        
          = 
         
         
          
          
            ( 
           
          
            z 
           
          
            − 
           
          
            2 
           
          
            x 
           
          
            ) 
           
          
            [ 
           
          
            − 
           
          
            2 
           
          
            x 
           
          
            + 
           
          
            z 
           
          
            ] 
           
          
          
          
            5 
           
          
         
        
          . 
         
        
       
         (curl F) \cdot n = (z - 2x)(x, -3y, z) \cdot \frac{(-2, 0, 1)}{\sqrt{5}} = \frac{(z - 2x)[-2x + z]}{\sqrt{5}}.
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mopen">
           (
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           c
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           u
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0278em;">
           r
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">
           lF
          </span>
          <span class="mclose">
           )
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mbin">
           ⋅
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           n
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mrel">
           =
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mopen">
           (
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.044em;">
           z
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mbin">
           −
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord">
           2
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           x
          </span>
          <span class="mclose">
           )
          </span>
          <span class="mopen">
           (
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           x
          </span>
          <span class="mpunct">
           ,
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord">

          <span class="mpunct">

          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">

          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.044em;">
           z
          </span>
          <span class="mclose">

          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">

    <p>
     注意到
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">

       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">

         </span>
         <span class="mord">

         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">

         </span>

         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.044em;">

         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">

         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>

     ，因此：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--display">
      <span class="katex-display">
       <span class="katex">

         (curl F) \cdot n = \frac{(z - 2x)^2}{\sqrt{5}}.
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">

     在
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        S 
        
       
      
        S
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>

     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">

         =

       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          2
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">

         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;">

         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.044em;">
          z
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          −
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          1
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          0
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     得
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        z 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         2 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         − 
        
       
         1 
        
       
      
        z = 2x - 1
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.044em;">
          z
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          2
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          −
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          1
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，故：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--display">
      <span class="katex-display">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         z 
         
        
          − 
         
        
          2 
         
        
          x 
         
        
          = 
         
        
          ( 
         
        
          2 
         
        
          x 
         
        
          − 
         
        
          1 
         
        
          ) 
         
        
          − 
         
        
          2 
         
        
          x 
         
        
          = 
         
        
          − 
         
        
          1 
         
         
        
          ⇒ 
         
         
        
          ( 
         
        
          z 
         
        
          − 
         
        
          2 
         
        
          x 
         
         
         
           ) 
          
         
           2 
          
         
        
          = 
         
        
          1. 
         
        
       
         z - 2x = (2x - 1) - 2x = -1 \quad \Rightarrow \quad (z - 2x)^2 = 1.
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.044em;">
           z
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mbin">
           −
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord">
           2
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           x
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mrel">
           =
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mopen">
           (
          </span>
          <span class="mord">
           2
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           x
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mbin">
           −
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord">
           1
          </span>
          <span class="mclose">
           )
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mbin">
           −
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord">
           2
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           x
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mrel">
           =
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord">
           −
          </span>
          <span class="mord">
           1
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mrel">
           ⇒
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mopen">
           (
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.044em;">
           z
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mbin">
           −
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 1.1141em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord">
           2
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           x
          </span>
          <span class="mclose">
           <span class="mclose">
            )
           </span>
           <span class="msupsub">
            <span class="vlist-t">
             <span class="vlist-r">
              <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8641em;">
               <span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                </span>
                <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  2
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mrel">
           =
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord">
           1.
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     因此，
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--display">
      <span class="katex-display">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         ( 
         
        
          c 
         
        
          u 
         
        
          r 
         
        
          l 
         
        
          F 
         
        
          ) 
         
        
          ⋅ 
         
        
          n 
         
        
          = 
         
         
         
           1 
          
          
          
            5 
           
          
         
         
        
          ( 
         
        
          为常数 
         
        
          ) 
         
        
          . 
         
        
       
         (curl F) \cdot n = \frac{1}{\sqrt{5}} \quad (为常数).
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mopen">
           (
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           c
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           u
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0278em;">
           r
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">
           lF
          </span>
          <span class="mclose">
           )
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mbin">
           ⋅
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           n
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mrel">
           =
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 2.2514em; vertical-align: -0.93em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mopen nulldelimiter">
           </span>
           <span class="mfrac">
            <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
             <span class="vlist-r">
              <span class="vlist" style="height: 1.3214em;">
               <span class="" style="top: -2.2028em;">
                <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;">
                </span>
                <span class="mord">
                 <span class="mord sqrt">
                  <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                   <span class="vlist-r">

    <p>
     故交圆的半径：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--display">
      <span class="katex-display">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         R 
         
        
          = 
         
         
          
          
            1 
           
          
            − 
           
           
           
             d 
            
           
             2 
            
           
          
         
        
          = 
         
         
          
          
            1 
           
          
            − 
           
           
           
             1 
            
           
             5 
            
           
          
         
        
          = 
         
         
          
          
            4 
           
          
            5 
           
          
         
        
          = 
         
         
         
           2 
          
          
          
            5 
           
          
         
        
          . 
         
        
       
         R = \sqrt{1 - d^2} = \sqrt{1 - \frac{1}{5}} = \sqrt{\frac{4}{5}} = \frac{2}{\sqrt{5}}.
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">

    <p>
     交圆在平面内的面积为

          . 
         
        
       
         Area(S) = \pi R^2 = \pi \left(\frac{4}{5}\right) = \frac{4\pi}{5}.
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">

    <p>
     【最终计算】
    </p>
    <p>
     由斯托克斯公式，
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--display">
      <span class="katex-display">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         ∮ 
          
         
           L 
          
         
        
          F 
         
        
          ⋅ 
         
        
          d 
         
        
          r 
         
        
          = 
         
         
         
           ∬ 
          
         
           S 
          
         
        
          ( 
         
        
          c 
         
        
          u 
         
        
          r 
         
        
          l 
         
        
          F 
         
        
          ) 
         
        
          ⋅ 
         
        
          n 
         
        
          d 
         
        
          S 
         
        
          = 
         
         
         
           ( 
          
          
          
            1 
           
           
           
             5 
            
           
          
         
           ) 
          
         
        
          × 
         
         
         
           ( 
          
          
           
           
             4 
            
           
             π 
            
           
          
            5 
           
          
         
           ) 
          
         
        
          = 
         
         
          
          
            4 
           
          
            π 
           
          
          
          
            5 
           
           
           
             5 
            
           
          
         
        
          . 
         
        
       
         \oint_L F \cdot dr = \iint_S (curl F) \cdot n dS = \left(\frac{1}{\sqrt{5}}\right) \times \left(\frac{4\pi}{5}\right) = \frac{4\pi}{5\sqrt{5}}.
        </span>

                        </path>
                       </svg>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <span class="vlist-s">

                   </span>
                   <span class="vlist-r">
                    <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1328em;">

               <span class="" style="top: -3.23em;">

    </p>

    <h3>
     <a id="_212">
     </a>
     数列问题
    </h3>
    <p>
     【问题描述】
    </p>
    <p>
     已知数列
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        { 
        
        
        
          x 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
         } 
        
       
      
        \{x_n\}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          {
          <!-- -->
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           x
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 n
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          }
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ,
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        { 
        
        
        
          y 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
         } 
        
       
      
        \{y_n\}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          {
          <!-- -->
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
           y
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0359em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 n
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          }
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ,
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        { 
        
        
        
          z 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
         } 
        
       
      
        \{z_n\}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          {
          <!-- -->
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.044em;">
           z
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.044em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 n
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          }
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     满足初值
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     x_0 = -1, \quad y_0 = 0, \quad z_0 = 2,
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     以及递推关系
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     x_n = -2x_{n-1} + 2z_{n-1},
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     y_n = -2y_{n-1} - 2z_{n-1},
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     z_n = -6x_{n-1} - 3y_{n-1} + 3z_{n-1}.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     令
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        α 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
         = 
        
        
        
          ( 
         
         
          
           
            
             
             
               x 
              
             
               n 
              
             
            
           
          
          
           
            
             
             
               y 
              
             
               n 
              
             
            
           
          
          
           
            
             
             
               z 
              
             
               n 
              
             
            
           
          
         
        
          ) 
         
        
       
      
        \alpha_n = \begin{pmatrix} x_n \\ y_n \\ z_n \end{pmatrix}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.5806em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">
           α
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0037em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 n
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 3.6em; vertical-align: -1.55em;">
         </span>
         <span class="minner">
          <span class="mopen">
           <span class="delimsizing mult">
            <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">

                </span>

                  <path d="M863,9c0,-2,-2,-5,-6,-9c0,0,-17,0,-17,0c-12.7,0,-19.3,0.3,-20,1

c0,-2.7,-3.3,-8.7,-10,-18c-135.3,-192.7,-235.5,-414.3,-300.5,-665c-65,-250.7,-102.5,

l0,-92c0,-162.7,5.7,-314,17,-454c20.7,-272,63.7,-513,129,-723c65.3,

            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="mclose">
           <span class="delimsizing mult">
            <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
             <span class="vlist-r">
              <span class="vlist" style="height: 2.05em;">
               <span class="" style="top: -4.05em;">
                <span class="pstrut" style="height: 5.6em;">
                </span>
                <span class="" style="width: 0.875em; height: 3.6em;">
                 <svg height="3.600em" viewbox="0 0 875 3600" width="0.875em">
                  <path d="M76,0c-16.7,0,-25,3,-25,9c0,2,2,6.3,6,13c21.3,28.7,42.3,60.3,

                  </path>
                 </svg>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span class="vlist-s">
               ​
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-r">
              <span class="vlist" style="height: 1.55em;">
               <span class="">
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，则有递推关系可写成
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     \alpha_n = A \alpha_{n-1}.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     问题要求：（1）写出矩阵
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        A 
        
       
      
        A
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          A
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ；（2）求
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        A 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
      
        A^n
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           A
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.6644em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 n
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     以及
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        x 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
      
        x_n
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.5806em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           x
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 n
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ,
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        y 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
      
        y_n
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
           y
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0359em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 n
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ,
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        z 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
      
        z_n
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.5806em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.044em;">
           z
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.044em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 n
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     的通项公式。
    </p>
    <p>
     【解】
    </p>
    <p>
     【第一步：构造矩阵
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        A 
        
       
      
        A
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          A
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     】
    </p>
    <p>
     由递推公式可知：
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     x_n = (-2)x_{n-1} + 0 \cdot y_{n-1} + 2z_{n-1},
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     y_n = 0 \cdot x_{n-1} + (-2)y_{n-1} + (-2)z_{n-1},
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     z_n = (-6)x_{n-1} + (-3)y_{n-1} + 3z_{n-1}.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     因此矩阵
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        A 
        
       
      
        A
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          A
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     即为
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     A = \begin{pmatrix} -2 &amp; 0 &amp; 2 \ 0 &amp; -2 &amp; -2 \ -6 &amp; -3 &amp; 3 \end{pmatrix}.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     【第二步：求
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        A 
        
       
      
        A
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          A
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     的
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        n 
        
       
      
        n
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          n
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     次幂
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        A 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
      
        A^n
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           A
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.6644em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 n
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     】
    </p>
    <p>
     为了求
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        A 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
      
        A^n
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           A
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.6644em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 n
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，我们采用对角化的方法。设
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        A 
        
       
      
        A
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          A
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     的特征值为
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        λ 
        
       
      
        \lambda
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          λ
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，求解
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        det 
        
       
         ⁡ 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         A 
        
       
         − 
        
       
         λ 
        
       
         I 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         0 
        
       
      
        \det(A - \lambda I) = 0
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mop">
          det
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          A
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          −
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          λ
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0785em;">
          I
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          0
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     。
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      写出
      <span class="katex--inline">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         A 
         
        
          − 
         
        
          λ 
         
        
          I 
         
        
       
         A - \lambda I
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           A
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mbin">
           −
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6944em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           λ
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0785em;">
           I
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
      ：
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     A - \lambda I = \begin{pmatrix} -2-\lambda &amp; 0 &amp; 2 \ 0 &amp; -2-\lambda &amp; -2 \ -6 &amp; -3 &amp; 3-\lambda \end{pmatrix}.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <ol start="2">
     <li>
      计算行列式：
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     \det(A - \lambda I)
    </p>
    <p>
     = (-2-\lambda) \cdot \det\begin{pmatrix} -2-\lambda &amp; -2 \ -3 &amp; 3-\lambda \end{pmatrix}
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      2 \cdot \det\begin{pmatrix} 0 &amp; -2-\lambda \ -6 &amp; -3 \end{pmatrix}.
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     其中
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     \det\begin{pmatrix} -2-\lambda &amp; -2 \ -3 &amp; 3-\lambda \end{pmatrix} = (-2-\lambda)(3-\lambda) - (-2)(-3)
    </p>
    <p>
     = (\lambda^2 - \lambda - 6) - 6 = \lambda^2 - \lambda - 12,
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     = (\lambda - 4)(\lambda + 3);
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     \det\begin{pmatrix} 0 &amp; -2-\lambda \ -6 &amp; -3 \end{pmatrix} = 0 \cdot (-3) - (-2-\lambda)(-6)
    </p>
    <p>
     = -6(\lambda+2).
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     因此，
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     \det(A - \lambda I) = (-2-\lambda)(\lambda-4)(\lambda+3) - 12(\lambda+2).
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     注意到
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        − 
        
       
         2 
        
       
         − 
        
       
         λ 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         − 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         λ 
        
       
         + 
        
       
         2 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        -2-\lambda = -(\lambda+2)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          −
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          2
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          −
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          λ
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          −
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          λ
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          +
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          2
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，可写为
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     \det(A - \lambda I) = - (\lambda+2)[(\lambda-4)(\lambda+3) + 12].
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     又有
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     (\lambda-4)(\lambda+3) = \lambda^2 - \lambda - 12, \quad 所以 \quad (\lambda-4)(\lambda+3) + 12 = \lambda^2 - \lambda.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     故，
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     \det(A - \lambda I) = - (\lambda+2) \lambda (\lambda-1) = 0.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     故矩阵
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        A 
        
       
      
        A
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          A
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     的特征值为：
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     \lambda_1 = 0, \quad \lambda_2 = 1, \quad \lambda_3 = -2.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     假设
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        A 
        
       
      
        A
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          A
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     可对角化，则存在可逆矩阵
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        P 
        
       
      
        P
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">
          P
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     和对角矩阵
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        D 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         diag 
        
       
         ⁡ 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         0 
        
       
         , 
        
       
         1 
        
       
         , 
        
       
         − 
        
       
         2 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        D = \operatorname{diag}(0, 1, -2)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0278em;">
          D
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mop">
          <span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.0139em;">
           diag
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          0
         </span>
         <span class="mpunct">
          ,
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          1
         </span>
         <span class="mpunct">
          ,
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          −
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          2
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，使得
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     A = P D P^{-1},
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     从而
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     A^n = P \cdot \operatorname{diag}(0^n, 1^n, (-2)^n) \cdot P^{-1}.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     【第三步：求
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        x 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
      
        x_n
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.5806em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
         </span>

    <p>
     ① 对于
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">

         =

       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">

         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">

         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ：
    </p>
    <p>
     解
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        ( 
        
       
         A

    <p>

    </p>
    <p>
     -2v_1 + 2v_3 = 0 \quad \Rightarrow \quad v_3 = v_1,
    </p>
    <p>

    </p>

    </p>

    </p>
    <p>

    </p>
    <p>

    </p>

    </p>

    </p>

      <span class="katex">

    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     v_{-2} = \begin{pmatrix} 1 \ -2 \ 0 \end{pmatrix}.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     令
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     \alpha_0 = c_0 \cdot v_0 + c_1 \cdot v_1 + c_{-2} \cdot v_{-2},
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     即：
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     \begin{pmatrix} -1 \ 0 \ 2 \end{pmatrix} = c_0 \cdot \begin{pmatrix} 1 \ -1 \ 1 \end{pmatrix} + c_1 \cdot \begin{pmatrix} 2 \ -2 \ 3 \end{pmatrix} + c_{-2} \cdot \begin{pmatrix} 1 \ -2 \ 0 \end{pmatrix}.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     分量方程为：
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     (1) \quad -1 = c_0 + 2c_1 + c_{-2},
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     (2) \quad 0 = - c_0 - 2c_1 - 2c_{-2},
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     (3) \quad 2 = c_0 + 3c_1.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     从 (3) 得
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">

              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 1

          <span class="msupsub">

               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  −
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  2
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2083em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          ⇒
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6389em; vertical-align: -0.2083em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           c
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  −
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  2
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2083em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          −
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          3
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          +
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.5806em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           c
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 1
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     .
    </p>
    <p>
     再代入 (2)：
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     0 = -(2 - 3c_1) - 2c_1 - 2(-3 + c_1)
    </p>
    <p>
     = -2 + 3c_1 - 2c_1 + 6 - 2c_1
    </p>
    <p>
     = 4 - c_1,
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     从而
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        c 
         
        
          1 
         
        
       
         = 
        
       
         4 
        
       
      
        c_1 = 4
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.5806em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           c
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 1
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          4
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     .
    </p>
    <p>
     进而，
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     c_0 = 2 - 3 \times 4 = -10, \quad c_{-2} = -3 + 4 = 1.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     因此，对于
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        n 
        
       
         ≥ 
        
       
         1 
        
       
      
        n \geq 1
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7719em; vertical-align: -0.136em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          n
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          ≥
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          1
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     （注意当
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        n 
        
       
         ≥ 
        
       
         1 
        
       
      
        n \geq 1
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7719em; vertical-align: -0.136em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          n
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          ≥
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          1
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     时，
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        0 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
         = 
        
       
         0 
        
       
      
        0^n = 0
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6644em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           0
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.6644em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 n
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          0
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ），有
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     \alpha_n = 4 \cdot v_1 + 1 \cdot (-2)^n \cdot v_{-2}.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     写出各分量，得：
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     x_n = 4 \times 2 + 1 \times (-2)^n = 8 + (-2)^n,
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     y_n = 4 \times (-2) + 1 \times (-2) \cdot (-2)^n = -8 - 2(-2)^n,
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     z_n = 4 \times 3 + 1 \times 0 = 12.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     （同时验证
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        n 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         0 
        
       
      
        n = 0
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          n
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          0
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     时：利用
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        0 
         
        
          0 
         
        
       
         = 
        
       
         1 
        
       
      
        0^0 = 1
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8141em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           0
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8141em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 0
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          1
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，得到 $x_0 = -10+8+1 = -1, y_0 = 10-8-2 = 0, z_0 = -10+12 = 2，与初值一致）
    </p>
    <p>
     【总结】
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      矩阵
      <span class="katex--inline">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         A 
         
        
       
         A
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           A
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
      为
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     A = \begin{pmatrix} -2 &amp; 0 &amp; 2 \ 0 &amp; -2 &amp; -2 \ -6 &amp; -3 &amp; 3 \end{pmatrix}.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <ol start="2">
     <li>
      <p>
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          A 
          
         
        
          A
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">
            A
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       的
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          n 
          
         
        
          n
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">
            n
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       次幂可表达为
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          A

           =
