           ⋅ 
          
          
          
            P 
           
           
           
             − 
            
           
             1 
            
           
          
         
        
          A^n = P \cdot \operatorname{diag}(0^n, 1, (-2)^n) \cdot P^{-1}
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mord mathnormal">
             A

            </span>
            <span class="msupsub">
             <span class="vlist-t">
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.6644em;">
                <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">

          </span>
          <span class="base">

            </span>
            <span class="msupsub">
             <span class="vlist-t">
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8141em;">
                <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mord mtight">
                   <span class="mord mtight">

                   </span>

          </span>

      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       数列通项（对于
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          n 
          
         
           ≥ 
          
         
           1 
          
         
        
          n \geq 1
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7719em; vertical-align: -0.136em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">
            n
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mrel">
            ≥
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            1
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       ）为：
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     x_n = 8 + (-2)^n,
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     y_n = -8 - 2(-2)^n,
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     z_n = 12.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <h3>
     <a id="_604">
     </a>
     估计问题
    </h3>
    <p>
     设总体
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        X 
        
       
      
        X
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0785em;">
          X
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     服从
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        [ 
        
       
         0 
        
       
         , 
        
       
         θ

       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">

         </span>
         <span class="mopen">

         </span>
         <span class="mord">

         </span>

         <span class="mrel">

         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">

         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          0
         </span>

     为未知参数，
    </p>

               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">

                 n
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">

             </span>

            <span class="vlist-r">

         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     是来自总体
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        X 
        
       
      
        X
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">

         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     的简单随机样本，记
    </p>
    <p>
     $ X(n) = \max { X_1, X_2, \cdots, X_n }, \quad T_c = cX(n). $
    </p>
    <p>
     (1) 求
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        c 
        
       
      
        c
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          c
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，使得
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        T 
         
        
          c 
         
        
       
      
        T_c
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">
           T
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.1389em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 c
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     是
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        θ 
        
       
      
        \theta
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0278em;">
          θ
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     的无偏估计；
    </p>
    <p>
     (2) 记
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        h 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         c 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         E 
        
       
         ( 
        
        
        
          T 
         
        
          c 
         
        
       
         − 
        
       
         θ 
        
        
        
          ) 
         
        
          2 
         
        
       
      
        h(c) = E(T_c - \theta)^2
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          h
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          c
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0576em;">
          E
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">
           T
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.1389em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 c
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          −
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1.0641em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0278em;">
          θ
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          <span class="mclose">
           )
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8141em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 2
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，求
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        c 
        
       
      
        c
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          c
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     使得
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        h 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         c 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        h(c)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          h
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          c
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     最小。
    </p>
    <p>
     —————— 解答 —————
    </p>
    <p>
     首先，由于
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        X 
         
        
          i 
         
        
       
         ∼ 
        
       
         U 
        
       
         ⁡ 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         0 
        
       
         , 
        
       
         θ 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        X_i \sim \operatorname{U}(0, \theta)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0785em;">
           X
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0785em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 i
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          ∼
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mop">
          <span class="mord mathrm">
           U
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          0
         </span>
         <span class="mpunct">
          ,
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0278em;">
          θ
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，记
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        Y 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         X 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         n 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        Y=X(n)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
          Y
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0785em;">
          X
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          n
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     为样本最大值，其累积分布函数为
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     F_Y(y) = \left(\frac{y}{\theta}\right)^n, \quad 0\le y\le\theta,
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     故其概率密度函数为
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     f_Y(y) = \frac{d}{dy}F_Y(y) = \frac{n}{\theta
     <sup>
      n}y
     </sup>
     {n-1}, \quad 0\le y\le\theta.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     【(1) 求无偏估计】
    </p>
    <p>
     计算
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        Y 
        
       
      
        Y
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
          Y
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     的均值：
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     E(Y) = \int_0^\theta y \frac{n}{\theta
     <sup>
      n}y
     </sup>
     {n-1},dy
    </p>
    <p>
     = \frac{n}{\theta
     <sup>
      n}\int_0
     </sup>
     \theta y^n,dy
    </p>
    <p>
     = \frac{n}{\theta^n} \cdot \frac{\theta^{n+1}}{n+1}
    </p>
    <p>
     = \frac{n}{n+1}\theta.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     由于估计量
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        T 
         
        
          c 
         
        
       
         = 
        
       
         c 
        
       
         Y 
        
       
      
        T_c = cY
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">
           T
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.1389em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 c
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          c
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
          Y
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     要无偏，即需满足
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     E(T_c)= cE(Y)= c\frac{n}{n+1}\theta = \theta,
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     从而解得
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     c = \frac{n+1}{n}.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     【(2) 求最小均方误差】
    </p>
    <p>
     计算均方误差：
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     h© = E[(cY-\theta)^2]
    </p>
    <p>
     = c
     <sup>
      2E(Y
     </sup>
     2) - 2c\theta E(Y) + \theta^2.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     同样地，可计算
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     E(Y^2) = \int_0^\theta y
     <sup>
      2\frac{n}{\theta
     </sup>
     n}y^{n-1},dy
    </p>
    <p>
     = \frac{n}{\theta
     <sup>
      n}\int_0
     </sup>
     \theta y^{n+1},dy
    </p>
    <p>
     = \frac{n}{\theta^n} \cdot \frac{\theta^{n+2}}{n+2}
    </p>
    <p>
     = \frac{n}{n+2}\theta^2.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     代入上式得
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     h© = c
     <sup>
      2\frac{n}{n+2}\theta
     </sup>
     2 - 2c\frac{n}{n+1}\theta^2 + \theta^2
    </p>
    <p>
     = \theta
     <sup>
      2\left(c
     </sup>
     2\frac{n}{n+2} - 2c\frac{n}{n+1} + 1\right).
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     令关于
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        c 
        
       
      
        c
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          c
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     的表达式取极值，对
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        c 
        
       
      
        c
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          c
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     求导并置零：
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     \frac{d}{dc} \left(c^2\frac{n}{n+2} - 2c\frac{n}{n+1} + 1\right)
    </p>
    <p>
     = 2c\frac{n}{n+2} - 2\frac{n}{n+1} = 0.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     解得
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     c = \frac{n+2}{n+1}.
    </p>
    <p>
     $$
    </p>
    <p>
     —————— 结论 —————
    </p>
    <p>

         <span class="mord mathnormal">

       </span>

     </span>
     ，则（ ）
    </p>
    <p>
     A.
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        f 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        f(x)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">

         </span>

         </span>

      </span>
     </span>
     是奇函数，
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        g

       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">

         </span>
         <span class="mopen">

         <span class="mclose">

         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     是偶函数
    </p>
    <p>
     B.
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        f 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        f(x)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1076em;">
          f
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     是偶函数，
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        g 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        g(x)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
          g
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     是奇函数
    </p>
    <p>
     C.
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        f 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        f(x)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1076em;">
          f
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     与
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        g 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         )

       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
          g
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     均为奇函数
    </p>
    <p>
     D.
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        f 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        f(x)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1076em;">
          f
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     与
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        g 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        g(x)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
          g
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">

         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     均为周期函数
    </p>
    <p>
     【解答过程】：
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       先判断
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          f 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           x 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
        
          f(x)
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1076em;">
            f
           </span>
           <span class="mopen">
            (
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">
            x
           </span>
           <span class="mclose">
            )
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       的性质：
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <p>
         <span class="katex--inline">
          <span class="katex">
           <span class="katex-mathml">
            f 
            
           
             ( 
            
           
             − 
            
           
             x 
            
           
             ) 
            
           
             = 
            
            
            
              ∫ 
             
            
              0 
             
             
             
               − 
              
             
               x 
              
             
            
            
            
              e 
             
             
             
               cos 
              
             
               ⁡ 
              
             
               t 
              
             
             
           
             d 
            
           
             t 
            
           
             = 
            
           
             − 
            
            
            
              ∫ 
             
            
              0 
             
            
              x 
             
            
            
            
              e 
             
             
             
               cos 
              
             
               ⁡ 
              
             
               ( 
              
             
               − 
              
             
               t 
              
             
               ) 
              
             
             
           
             d 
            
           
             t 
            
           
             = 
            
           
             − 
            
            
            
              ∫ 
             
            
              0 
             
            
              x 
             
            
            
            
              e 
             
             
             
               cos 
              
             
               ⁡ 
              
             
               t 
              
             
             
           
             d 
            
           
             t 
            
           
             = 
            
           
             − 
            
           
             f 
            
           
             ( 
            
           
             x 
            
           
             ) 
            
           
          
            f(-x) = \int_0^{-x} e^{\cos t} \, dt = -\int_0^x e^{\cos (-t)} \, dt = -\int_0^x e^{\cos t} \, dt = -f(x)
           </span>
           <span class="katex-html">
            <span class="base">
             <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
             </span>

             </span>

             <span class="mop">
              <span class="mop op-symbol small-op" style="margin-right: 0.1945em; position: relative; top: -0.0006em;">

            </span>
            <span class="base">
             <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
             </span>
             <span class="mord">

             </span>
             <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1076em;">

             </span>
             <span class="mopen">

          </span>
         </span>
        </p>
       </li>
       <li>
        <p>
         因此，
         <span class="katex--inline">
          <span class="katex">
           <span class="katex-mathml">
            f 
            
           
             ( 
            
           
             x 
            
           
             ) 
            
           
          
            f(x)
           </span>
           <span class="katex-html">
            <span class="base">
             <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
             </span>
             <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1076em;">
              f
             </span>
             <span class="mopen">
              (
             </span>
             <span class="mord mathnormal">
              x
             </span>
             <span class="mclose">
              )
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         是奇函数。
        </p>
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       再判断
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          g 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           x 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
        
          g(x)
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
            g
           </span>
           <span class="mopen">
            (
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">
            x
           </span>
           <span class="mclose">
            )
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       的性质：
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <p>
         <span class="katex--inline">
          <span class="katex">
           <span class="katex-mathml">
            g 
            
           
             ( 
            
           
             − 
            
           
             x 
            
           
             ) 
            
           
             = 
            
            
            
              ∫ 
             
            
              0 
             
             
             
               sin 
              
             
               ⁡ 
              
             
               ( 
              
             
               − 
              
             
               x 
              
             
               ) 
              
             
            
            
            
              e 
             
             
             
               t 
              
             
               2 
              
             
             
           
             d 
            
           
             t 
            
           
             = 
            
            
            
              ∫ 
             
            
              0 
             
             
             
               − 
              
             
               sin 
              
             
               ⁡ 
              
             
               x 
              
             
            
            
            
              e 
             
             
             
               t 
              
             
               2 
              
             
             
           
             d 
            
           
             t 
            
           
             = 
            
           
             − 
            
            
            
              ∫ 
             
            
              0 
             
             
             
               sin 
              
             
               ⁡ 
              
             
               x 
              
             
            
            
            
              e 
             
             
             
               t 
              
             
               2 
              
             
             
           
             d 
            
           
             t 
            
           
             = 
            
           
             − 
            
           
             g 
            
           
             ( 
            
           
             x 
            
           
             ) 
            
           
          
            g(-x) = \int_0^{\sin (-x)} e^{t^2} \, dt = \int_0^{-\sin x} e^{t^2} \, dt = -\int_0^{\sin x} e^{t^2} \, dt = -g(x)
           </span>
           <span class="katex-html">
            <span class="base">
             <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
             </span>
             <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
              g
             </span>
             <span class="mopen">
              (
             </span>
             <span class="mord">
              −
             </span>
             <span class="mord mathnormal">

             </span>
             <span class="mclose">

             </span>
             <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">

             <span class="mop">
              <span class="mop op-symbol small-op" style="margin-right: 0.1945em; position: relative; top: -0.0006em;">
               ∫
              </span>
              <span class="msupsub">
               <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                <span class="vlist-r">
                 <span class="vlist" style="height: 1.0829em;">
                  <span class="" style="top: -2.3442em; margin-left: -0.1945em; margin-right: 0.05em;">

                   <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                    <span class="mord mtight">

                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span class="" style="top: -3.2579em; margin-right: 0.05em;">

                   <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                    <span class="mord mtight">
                     <span class="mop mtight">
                      <span class="mtight">
                       s

                      <span class="mtight">
                       i
                      </span>
                      <span class="mtight">
                       n
                      </span>
                     </span>
                     <span class="mopen mtight">

                 <span class="vlist-s">

                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
             </span>
             <span class="mord">
              <span class="mord mathnormal">
               e
              </span>
              <span class="msupsub">
               <span class="vlist-t">
                <span class="vlist-r">
                 <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.9869em;">
                  <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                   <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                   </span>
                   <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                    <span class="mord mtight">
                     <span class="mord mtight">
                      <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                       t
                      </span>
                      <span class="msupsub">
                       <span class="vlist-t">

     综上所述，正确答案是 C.
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        f 
        
       
         (

         </span>

     均为奇函数。
